DROP TABLE COMMENT;
DROP TABLE QUES;
DROP TABLE CAREER;
DROP TABLE APPLY;
DROP TABLE SELFINTRO;
DROP TABLE REVIEWBOARD;
DROP TABLE LICENSE;
DROP TABLE LANGUAGE;
DROP TABLE RESUME;
DROP TABLE CHATBOT;
DROP TABLE MEMBER;
DROP TABLE CRAWLING;
DROP TABLE INCRUIT;
DROP TABLE PASSBOARD;
DROP TABLE UNIVERSITY;
DROP TABLE MAJOR;

create table INCRUIT(
   CO_SEQ int(100) AUTO_INCREMENT , 
   CO_NAME varchar(1000), 
   CO_NAME_HREF varchar(1000), 
   CO_TITLE varchar(1000),
   CO_JOB_MID_NAME varchar(1000),
   CO_JOB_NAME varchar(1000),
   CO_LOCATION_NAME varchar(1000),
   CO_CAREER varchar(1000),
   CO_START_DATE DATE,
   CO_END_DATE DATE,
   CO_READ_COUNT int(11),
   CO_URL varchar(1000),
   CO_SALARY varchar(1000),
   CO_JOB_TYPE varchar(1000),
   CO_EDUCATION varchar(1000),
   PRIMARY KEY(CO_SEQ)
);
#insert into INCRUIT(CO_SEQ) values (1);

create table MEMBER(
   U_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT, 
   U_ID varchar(1000), 
   U_PASSWORD varchar(1000), 
   U_NAME varchar(1000),
   U_GENDER varchar(1000),
   U_BIRTH varchar(1000),
   U_JOB varchar(1000),
   U_DEGREE varchar(1000),
   U_EMAIL varchar(1000),
   U_MAJOR varchar(1000),
   U_PHONE varchar(1000),
   U_CAREER varchar(1000),
   U_PROVIDER varchar(1000),
   isManager varchar(1000),
   U_LASTSCHOOL varchar(1000),
   U_MemberSince DATE,
   PRIMARY KEY (U_SEQ)
);
#insert into MEMBER(U_SEQ) values (1);

create table SELFINTRO(
   SELF_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   U_SEQ int(10),
   SELF_NAME varchar(1000),
   APPLY_CHECK boolean default false,
   PRIMARY KEY (SELF_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES MEMBER(U_SEQ)
);
#insert into SELFINTRO(SELF_SEQ,U_SEQ,CO_SEQ) values(1,1,1);
#insert into SELFINTRO(SELF_SEQ,U_SEQ,CO_SEQ) values(2,1,1);

create table QUES(
   QA_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   SELF_SEQ int(10),
   QA_Q varchar(4000),
   QA_A varchar(12000),
   PRIMARY KEY (QA_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (SELF_SEQ) REFERENCES SELFINTRO(SELF_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);
#insert into QUES(QA_SEQ,SELF_SEQ,QA_Q,QA_A) values (1,1,'일어나세요','치영님');
#insert into QUES(QA_SEQ,SELF_SEQ,QA_Q,QA_A) values (2,1,'일어나세요','동원님');
#insert into QUES(QA_SEQ,SELF_SEQ,QA_Q,QA_A) values (3,1,'일어나세요','동연님');

create table REVIEWBOARD(
   REVIEW_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   U_SEQ int(10),
   COMPANY_NAME varchar(1000).
   REVIEW_TITLE varchar(1000),
   REVIEW_CONTENT varchar(1000),
   REVIEW_DATE DATE,
   PASS_HIT int(10) default 0,
   PRIMARY KEY (REVIEW_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES MEMBER(U_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);
SET foreign_key_checks = 0;
alter table reviewboard drop constraint reviewboard_ibfk_2;
SET foreign_key_checks = 1;
alter table reviewboard change co_seq company_name varchar(1000);

create table COMMENT(
   COMMENT_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   REVIEW_SEQ int(10),
   U_SEQ int(10),
   COMMENT_CONTENT varchar(1000),
   PRIMARY KEY (COMMENT_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (REVIEW_SEQ) REFERENCES REVIEWBOARD(REVIEW_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE,
   FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES REVIEWBOARD(U_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

create table RESUME(
   RE_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   U_SEQ int(10),
   RE_ZIPCODE varchar(1000),
   RE_ADDRESS varchar(1000),
   RE_HIGH varchar(500),   
   RE_HIGHSTATUS varchar(1000),
   RE_HIGHSTARTDATE DATE,
   RE_HIGHENDDATE DATE,
   RE_UNIV varchar(500),
   RE_UNIVSTATUS varchar(1000),
   RE_UNIVSDATE DATE,
   RE_UNIVEDATE DATE,
   RE_UNIVGRADE varchar(1000),
   RE_UNIVMAJOR varchar(1000),
   RE_MASTER varchar(500),
   RE_MASTERSTATUS varchar(1000),
   RE_MASTERSDATE DATE,
   RE_MASTEREDATE DATE,
   RE_MASTERGRADE varchar(1000),
   RE_MASTERMAJOR varchar(1000),
   RE_STATUS varchar(500),
   RE_NAME varchar(500) default null,
   RE_BIRTH varchar(500) default null,
   RE_GENDER varchar(500) default null,
   RE_PHONE varchar(500) default null,
   RE_EMAIL varchar(500) default null,
   RE_HIGHMAJOR varchar(500) default null,
   RE_MILITARY varchar(100) default null,
   RE_TITLE varchar(500) default null,
   RE_PIC varchar(500),
   APPLY_CHECK boolean default false,
   PRIMARY KEY (RE_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES MEMBER(U_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

create table CAREER(
   CA_SEQ int(10) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   RE_SEQ int(10),
   CA_CO_NAME varchar(1000),
   CA_POSITION varchar(1000),
   CA_START DATE,
   CA_END DATE,
   CA_DURATION varchar(1000),
   CA_DEPT varchar(1000),
   CA_WORK varchar(1000),
   PRIMARY KEY (CA_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (RE_SEQ) REFERENCES RESUME(RE_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

create table LICENSE(
   LI_SEQ int(10) not null auto_increment,
   LI_NAME varchar(100),
   RE_SEQ int(10),
   LI_AGENCY varchar(1000),
   LI_DATE varchar(1000),
   PRIMARY KEY(LI_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (RE_SEQ) REFERENCES RESUME(RE_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

create table LANGUAGE(
   LA_SEQ int(10) not null auto_increment,
   LA_TEST_NAME varchar(100),
   RE_SEQ int(10),
   LA_SCORE varchar(1000),
   LA_DATE varchar(1000),
   PRIMARY KEY(LA_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (RE_SEQ) REFERENCES RESUME(RE_SEQ) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

create table PASSBOARD(
   PASS_SEQ int(11) AUTO_INCREMENT,
   PASS_TITLE varchar(100),
   PASS_COMPANY varchar(100),
   PASS_CAREER varchar(100),
   PASS_JOB varchar(100),
   PASS_UNIV varchar(100),
   PASS_GRADE varchar(100),
   PASS_TOEIC varchar(100),
   PASS_CONTENT varchar(12000),
   PASS_HIT int(10) default 0,
   PRIMARY KEY(PASS_SEQ)
);

create table CRAWLING(
    CL_SEQ int(100) not null auto_increment,
    CO_SEQ int(100),
    CL_recruitment TEXT(12000),
    CL_workingconditions TEXT(12000),
    CL_screeningproce TEXT(12000),
    CL_applicationperiod TEXT(12000),
    CL_notice TEXT(12000),
    CL_IMG TEXT(12000),
    CL_LOGO TEXT(12000),
    CL_IFRAME MEDIUMBLOB default null,
    CL_STATUS varchar(100),
    PRIMARY KEY (CL_SEQ),
    FOREIGN KEY (CO_SEQ) REFERENCES INCRUIT(CO_SEQ)
);

create table CHATBOT(
   U_SEQ int(10),
   INTERVIEW_SEQ int(10),
   CHAT_SEQ int(10) auto_increment,
   CHAT_Q varchar(1000),
   CHAT_A varchar(1000),
   CHAT_DATE DATE,
   PRIMARY KEY(CHAT_SEQ),
   FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES MEMBER(U_SEQ)
); 

create table APPLY(
  U_SEQ int(10),
  CO_SEQ int(10),
  APPLY_DATE DATE,
  RE_SEQ int(10),
  SELF_SEQ int(10),
  APPLY_READCHECK tinyint(1) default 0,
  FOREIGN KEY (U_SEQ) REFERENCES MEMBER(U_SEQ),
  FOREIGN KEY (CO_SEQ) REFERENCES INCRUIT(CO_SEQ),
  FOREIGN KEY (RE_SEQ) REFERENCES RESUME(RE_SEQ),
  FOREIGN KEY (SELF_SEQ) REFERENCES SELFINTRO(SELF_SEQ)
);

create table UNIVERSITY(
    UNIV_NAME varchar(500),
    primary key (UNIV_NAME)
);

create table MAJOR(
    MAJOR_NAME varchar(500),
    primary key (MAJOR_NAME)
);
